{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2021-04-03 12:49:31","updatedTime":"2021-04-03 12:49:31","title":"Hide a cat litter box in a STUVA bench","link":"https://www.ikeahackers.net/?p=82643","description":"<span class=\"cb-itemprop\" itemprop=\"reviewBody\">\n<p>I wanted to hide the cat litter box in a piece of furniture such as the STUVA bench, but I did not want to do anything too complicated. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>I also hoped that this way most of the litter stuck on my cat&#8217;s paw will remain inside. Additionally, it may help with the odour.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>IKEA items used: </h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li><a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/tag/stuva\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">STUVA</a> 90x50x50</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"884\" height=\"874\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/Stuva-bench.jpg\" alt=\"STUVA toy storage\" class=\"wp-image-75793\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/Stuva-bench.jpg 884w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/Stuva-bench-550x544.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/Stuva-bench-768x759.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/Stuva-bench-125x125.jpg 125w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 884px) 100vw, 884px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">STUVA bench | IKEA.com</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Other materials and tools: </h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>Sandpaper</li><li>Paint (optional)</li><li>Adhesive hooks (optional)</li><li>Drill  </li><li>Saber saw </li></ul>\n\n\n\n<h3>STUVA bench cat litter box instructions: </h3>\n\n\n\n<p>1. Use a bowl or a plate to draw a big circle on the front of the drawer. It&#8217;s easier to do this before assembly.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"497\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/cat-litter-stuva-bench-2.jpg\" alt=\"draw circle \" class=\"wp-image-82644\"/></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-luminous-vivid-orange-color has-text-color\"><strong>Related:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2016/07/easy-clean-stuva-bench-litter-box.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Easy to Clean Stuva Bench Litter Box</a></p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<p>2. Use a drill to make a hole next to the line (inside the circle) big enough for the saw. Then insert the saw into the hole and cut out the circle.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"782\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/cat-litter-stuva-bench-3-1.jpg\" alt=\"cut circle\" class=\"wp-image-82646\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/cat-litter-stuva-bench-3-1.jpg 782w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/cat-litter-stuva-bench-3-1-550x720.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/cat-litter-stuva-bench-3-1-768x1006.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 782px) 100vw, 782px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>3. Use sandpaper to sand the circle and get rid of any possible splinters. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>4. Assemble the front to the rest of the bench.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"497\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/cat-litter-stuva-bench.jpg\" alt=\"bench cat litter box stuva\" class=\"wp-image-82647\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/cat-litter-stuva-bench.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/cat-litter-stuva-bench-550x267.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/cat-litter-stuva-bench-768x373.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"575\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/stuva-bench-cat-litter.jpg\" alt=\"bench cat litter box stuva\" class=\"wp-image-82648\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/stuva-bench-cat-litter.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/stuva-bench-cat-litter-550x309.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/stuva-bench-cat-litter-768x431.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Optionally, you can use paint to draw something around the hole. It is certainly not necessary, but it helps hide any possible unevenness. (I recommend using a primer first). I also added some adhesive hooks for the <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://amzn.to/3ePxj78\" target=\"_blank\">shovel</a> and bags.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"620\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/stuva-bench-cat-litter-4.jpg\" alt=\"bench cat litter box IKEA stuva\" class=\"wp-image-82649\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/stuva-bench-cat-litter-4.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/stuva-bench-cat-litter-4-550x333.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/stuva-bench-cat-litter-4-768x465.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-luminous-vivid-orange-color has-text-color\"><strong>Related:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2017/06/diy-hidden-cat-litter-station.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Spoiled kitty comfort station hidden in mudroom space</a></p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<h5>How long and how much did it cost? </h5>\n\n\n\n<p>I bought the STUVA second hand for 30€ (not sure what it used to cost since it is not in the catalog anymore). The <a href=\"https://fave.co/2Q4Pnj4\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">SMÅSTAD bench</a> 90x52x48 (69€ now) is pretty similar.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>What to pay special attention to? </h5>\n\n\n\n<p>If you use the drill too close to the line you may end up with an uneven circle. Also, make sure the cat litter box will fit inside the STUVA bench, because I only thought about the outside measurements and my litter box ended up being only a few centimeters short of not fitting in. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Hope this is useful for someone!</p>\n\n\n\n<p>by Nerea</p>\n</span><p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2021/03/cat-litter-box-stuva-bench.html\">Hide itemprop=\"reviewBody\">\n<p>Installing the IKEA <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/tag/moppe\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">MOPPE</a> mini chest of drawers in the <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/tag/ivar\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IVAR</a> side unit. Very easy to do. No glue or screws needed.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>IKEA items used: </h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>8 IVAR metal rods 40 x 6 mm (comes with the <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://fave.co/38Tbkbp\" target=\"_blank\">IVAR shelves</a>)</li><li>1 <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://fave.co/3cC6qAA\" target=\"_blank\">IKEA MOPPE mini chest of drawers</a> 42 x 32 cm</li><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://fave.co/2VpnO3F\" target=\"_blank\">IVAR side unit</a> (50cm depth)</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<h3>How to add mini drawers to IVAR side unit</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Make 4 x 6mm holes on each side of the IKEA MOPPE box.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The top two pair of holes are situated 3.2 mm from the top edge and 2.7 mm apart.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-drawers-ivar-system.jpg\" alt=\"metal rods\" class=\"wp-image-82653\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-drawers-ivar-system.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-drawers-ivar-system-550x550.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-drawers-ivar-system-150x150.jpg 150w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-drawers-ivar-system-768x768.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-drawers-ivar-system-125x125.jpg 125w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-luminous-vivid-orange-color has-text-color\"><strong>Related:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2021/01/folding-screen-ikea-ivar.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">8 ways to turn IVAR into a super useful folding screen</a></p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<p>I prefer centered for balance. But that is flexible.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>They should fit the holes in the IVAR system.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" made them 25.7 mm below. 3.2 mm from the bottom edge.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Do remove the drawers before drilling the holes.</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"1573\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ivar-with-moppe-drawers.jpg\" alt=\"ivar mini drawers\" class=\"wp-image-82655\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ivar-with-moppe-drawers.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ivar-with-moppe-drawers-550x845.jpg 550w, sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>Push the rods from the inside through the new holes and into the IVAR holes on the side unit.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"1024\" itemprop=\"reviewBody\">\n<p>The IKEA IVAR cabinet is so easy to customise with paint. Give it a mono-colour or give it as many as you like. </p>\n\n\n\n<h3>#1 Karoline&#8217;s colorful IVAR cabinet paint hack&#160;</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>I wanted to create a really colourful piece of furniture. I love that the <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/tag/ivar\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IVAR</a> cabinets are solid wood so they are so nice and easy to paint – and the simple design is amazing.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>IKEA item:</h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>6 IKEA <a href=\"https://fave.co/2PSUS4j\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IVAR cabinets</a>&#160;</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"750\" height=\"500\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/ikea-ivar-with-doors-engraved.jpg\" alt=\"ikea-ivar-cabinet\" class=\"wp-image-78649\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/ikea-ivar-with-doors-engraved.jpg 750w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/ikea-ivar-with-doors-engraved-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/ikea-ivar-with-doors-engraved-360x240.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Photo: IKEA.com</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Other materials:</h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>Wood paint and acrylic paint in different colors&#160;</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>Just lots of colourful paint. The IVAR cabinets are so great, and I look forward to see all the different ways to repaint and remake them in the future.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"767\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/IMG_4947-Kopi.jpg\" alt=\"acrylic paint\" class=\"wp-image-82631\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/IMG_4947-Kopi.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/IMG_4947-Kopi-550x412.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/IMG_4947-Kopi-768x575.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"772\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/IMG_4957-Kopi.jpg\" alt=\"assembly\" class=\"wp-image-82632\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/IMG_4957-Kopi.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/IMG_4957-Kopi-550x415.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/IMG_4957-Kopi-768x579.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>It cost the cost of the IVAR cabinets (440 dollars), and the paint was all I had leftover in my stash. New paint in all these colours could be 150 dollars, but you can also be lucky to find cheap paint samples or mix your own like I did.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"767\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/IMG_5014-Kopi.jpg\" alt=\"ivar cabinet paint\" class=\"wp-image-82633\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/IMG_5014-Kopi.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/IMG_5014-Kopi-550x412.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/IMG_5014-Kopi-768x575.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>It took an afternoon to do, and I loved every bit of the process. We had fun assembling them and building them up on the wall. And the painting process was so much fun.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>See the <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://skandimama.com/best-ikea-ivar-hack/\" target=\"_blank\">complete tutorial on my blog</a> or watch the video below.</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-embed-youtube wp-block-embed is-type-video is-provider-youtube wp-embed-aspect-16-9 wp-has-aspect-ratio\"><div class=\"wp-block-embed__wrapper\">\n<iframe title=\"Best IKEA Ivar hack\" width=\"1200\" height=\"675\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/op1UXLhSOiI?feature=oembed\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen></iframe>\n</div></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>~ by Karoline Dahrling Hughes</p>\n\n\n\n<h3>#2 Emilie&#8217;s stylish terracotta cabinet</h3>\n\n\n\n<h5>IKEA item:</h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>IKEA IVAR cabinet</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<h5>Other materials and tools:</h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>4 x <a href=\"https://amzn.to/30LNpGq\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">legs</a></li><li>2 x <a href=\"https://amzn.to/30GycGz\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">handles</a></li><li>Paint in desired colour</li><li>Drill</li><li>Paint roller</li><li>Paint brush</li><li>Screwdriver</li><li>Hammer</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>Paint the whole cabinets with a small roller and use paint brush for smaller and tricky to reach areas. </p>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>Tip:</strong> Open the doors slightly to reach the side of the side panels. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Pencil the location of the leg holes, make a guide indent with a hammer and nail, screw on legs using a screwdriver. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ivar-studio-cabinet-2-rotated.jpg\" alt=\"brass legs\" class=\"wp-image-82634\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ivar-studio-cabinet-2-rotated.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ivar-studio-cabinet-2-550x733.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Drill a hole in the position you would like the handles, I put them at the top for ease. Secure handles with screws.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ivar-studio-cabinet-1-rotated.jpg\" alt=\"handles\" class=\"wp-image-82635\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ivar-studio-cabinet-1-rotated.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ivar-studio-cabinet-1-550x733.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>I bought the cabinet in Spain for €59, <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://amzn.to/30LNpGq\" target=\"_blank\">brass/gold legs on&#160;Amazon</a>&#160;for €35.99, <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://amzn.to/30GycGz\" target=\"_blank\">brass/gold handles from&#160;Amazon</a>&#160;for €9.79. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>And I found the paint in the street, as a decorating firm were throwing away lots of paints. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ivar-studio-cabinet-3-rotated.jpg\" alt=\"paint\" class=\"wp-image-82636\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ivar-studio-cabinet-3-rotated.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ivar-studio-cabinet-3-550x733.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>I found one that matched back to a print I had on our studio wall so it was perfect and felt good recycling unwanted paint. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>As the cabinet was for a office I needed to find legs tall enough to store our printer underneath. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ivar-studio-cabinet-4-rotated.jpg\" alt=\"ivar cabinet paint\" https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ivar-studio-cabinet-4-550x733.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>When open, the cabinet is a jewellery makers dream, full of sparkling and golden components. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" 12:49:31","updatedTime":"2021-04-03 12:49:31","title":"Using the LACK table as a canvas for art","link":"https://www.ikeahackers.net/?p=82741","description":"<span class=\"cb-itemprop\" itemprop=\"reviewBody\">\n<p>The IKEA <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/tag/lack\" target=\"_blank\">LACK</a> table is like an art canvas to me. And they are cheaper than canvas. It is also easy to transport between exhibitions or when sending to clients. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>You can also use them as tables. Or as paintings, if you screw off the legs and hang them on the wall.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>This is a 90x50x45 cm LACK coffee table I used for expressing a view of my life in Sweden, which I sum up as &#8230;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Life can be hard. Depending in where you live, the struggle of surviving varies. Living in Sweden is easier than in many other countries, even though you see “darkness” and feel “stuck” there are always paths to take you out of trouble. And all problems become like paths surrounded with beautiful cactuses.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5><strong>IKEA items:</strong> </h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li><a href=\"https://fave.co/3pLJowm\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">LACK coffee table</a> 90x55x45 cm</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"500\" height=\"500\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/11/lack-coffee-table__57540_PE163122_S4.jpg\" alt=\"Lack coffee table\" class=\"wp-image-23561\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/11/lack-coffee-table__57540_PE163122_S4.jpg 500w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/11/lack-coffee-table__57540_PE163122_S4-150x150.jpg 150w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/11/lack-coffee-table__57540_PE163122_S4-300x300.jpg 300w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/11/lack-coffee-table__57540_PE163122_S4-50x50.jpg 50w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/11/lack-coffee-table__57540_PE163122_S4-186x186.jpg 186w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Photo: <a href=\"https://fave.co/3pLJowm\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IKEA.com</a></p>\n\n\n\n<h5><strong>Other materials:</strong> </h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>CD-ROM pieces painted with alcohol ink </li><li>Acrylic paint </li><li>Resin</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<h3>How I created my LACK table art<strong>: </strong></h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Recycling materials by using them in my creations is something I like to do. In this case I used old CD-ROM discs.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"679\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/CD-ROM–pieces.jpg\" alt=\"cd rom pieces\" class=\"wp-image-82742\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/CD-ROM–pieces.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/CD-ROM–pieces-550x365.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/CD-ROM–pieces-768x509.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/CD-ROM–pieces-100x65.jpg 100w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/CD-ROM–pieces-360x240.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>I started cutting the discs in different shapes and colored with alcohol inks.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>After deciding a composition, I glued the pieces on the table. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"645\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/glued-CD.jpg\" alt=\"table art IKEA LACK hack\" class=\"wp-image-82743\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/glued-CD.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/glued-CD-550x346.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/glued-CD-768x484.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Than, I poured black resin on the table and around the disc pieces.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"642\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/black-resin.jpg\" alt=\"resin\" class=\"wp-image-82744\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/black-resin.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/black-resin-550x345.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/black-resin-768x482.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Next day, I sanded the black resin and poured a new layer of transparent resin and let it to cure for at least 12 hours.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>I sanded again the resin, painted lines and dots with an acrylic pen and poured a new layer of transparent resin.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/sand-and-lines.jpg\" alt=\"table art IKEA LACK hack\" class=\"wp-image-82745\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/sand-and-lines.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/sand-and-lines-550x413.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/sand-and-lines-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Now I had to let the resin cure for week in able to cure hard. Last but not least, I screwed the legs.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"682\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/The-Path-to-Joy-is-Surrounded-with-Beautiful-Swedish-Cactuses-.jpg\" alt=\"table art IKEA LACK hack\" class=\"wp-image-82746\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/The-Path-to-Joy-is-Surrounded-with-Beautiful-Swedish-Cactuses-.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/The-Path-to-Joy-is-Surrounded-with-Beautiful-Swedish-Cactuses--550x366.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/The-Path-to-Joy-is-Surrounded-with-Beautiful-Swedish-Cactuses--768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/The-Path-to-Joy-is-Surrounded-with-Beautiful-Swedish-Cactuses--360x240.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>The resin can withstand up to 50 ° C, if small scratches appear, polish the table with car polish, if the scratches are deep, the surface must be sanded with fine sandpaper to then pour a new layer of resin.&#160;All colours fade over time, to prolong the life of the colours, do not expose the table directly under sunlight for long periods of time.</p>\n\n\n\n<p><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://gaines.se/the-path-to-joy-is-surrounded-with-beautiful-swedish-cactuses/\" target=\"_blank\">Link to my blog with the work process.</a></p>\n\n\n\n<p>~ Ana border=\"0\"></img></a>\n</div><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/Ikeahacker/~4/9Juel23lgpA\" height=\"1\" width=\"1\" alt=\"\"/>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Wed, 10 Mar 2021 14:00:50 +0000","feedId":65,"bgimg":"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/effektiv.jpg","linkMd5":"97a650ea2054bfce59577a49a7824c19","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx19/cdn30@2020_1/2021/04/03/04-49-32-580_39ec050f40f4a444.webp","destWidth":768,"destHeight":1024,"sourceBytes":199531,"destBytes":84578,"author":"Contributor","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/effektiv.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx19/cdn30@2020_1/2021/04/03/04-49-32-580_39ec050f40f4a444.webp","https://ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/blogger/-S1K-hMpcsNk/Tov88XW1wHI/AAAAAAAATOg/T8zfiiqIYac/s640/1-Foto0078-705415.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn27@2020_5/2021/04/03/04-49-55-052_875e04abba99666c.webp","https://ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/blogger/-wNsdTomz1uI/Tov88tQ8mnI/AAAAAAAATOo/6cZu9z26PWo/s640/1-Foto0079-706477.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx31/cdn62@2020_2/2021/04/03/04-49-55-278_c28a1c2e5b5fa570.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/Ikeahacker?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn19@2020_4/2021/04/03/04-49-54-527_05353866f732d1c2.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/Ikeahacker?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx13/cdn71@2020_3/2021/04/03/04-49-53-457_1b4a6100740437d6.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/Ikeahacker?i=9Juel23lgpA:CU-0PAPnxGs:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx13/cdn89@2020_6/2021/04/03/04-49-53-395_3ac9ae8c5f80748c.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/Ikeahacker/~4/9Juel23lgpA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn76@2020_4/2021/04/03/04-49-55-098_d2bc408300bd3c46.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1617425371957},{"createdTime":"2021-04-03 12:49:31","updatedTime":"2021-04-03 12:49:31","title":"Elegant Next Bed Murphy Bed in a PAX wardrobe","link":"https://www.ikeahackers.net/?p=82661","description":"<span class=\"cb-itemprop\" itemprop=\"reviewBody\">\n<p class=\"has-medium-font-size\"><em>DIY Murphy Bed using a Next Bed Murphy Bed Kit and IKEA PAX wardrobe cabinets.</em></p>\n\n\n\n<p>While our daughter was away at university, we relied on her room as a guest room. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>When <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2020/11/mask-storage-hacks.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">COVID struck</a>, our daughter moved back home full time, so we lost our guest room in the process. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>We don’t have a constant flow of guests in and out of our home, but we have enough visitors where we needed to come up with a suitable solution.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>We decided to turn my home office into our new temporary guest room.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Wasting space on a queen size bed that is only seldomly in use was not ideal, and occasionally conducting client meetings in my office, having a bed in full view was completely out of the question. This is where the idea of a Murphy bed came into play.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>I called around for quotes. And was surprised at how much carpenters were charging to build a Murphy bed. I figured that I could build one myself. So, I found the following inspiration photos on www.houzz.com and set about designing and building my own.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Found! The Next Bed Murphy Bed</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>I researched quite a bit for Murphy bed hardware and came across the <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://fave.co/38RuEWF\" target=\"_blank\">Next Bed Murphy Bed Kit</a>. The appealing thing I found with the Next Bed Murphy Bed kit is that unlike in a traditional Murphy Bed, the Next Bed is not built into the cabinet.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>It is a stand-alone piece of equipment. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Since the Next Bed attaches directly to your wall, it doesn’t rely on structural support from the cabinet in order to operate properly. This meant that my cabinet would purely be a decorative cover used to hide the bed.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>In order to keep the costs down, I kept things as standard as possible. Doors are the most expensive item in cabinetry, so custom-building doors was out of the question. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>My bed is a queen size 150cm x 200cm, and the kit stated that I needed a minimum of 160cm for properly installing the murphy bed. So I combined 2 100cm wide <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/tag/pax\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">PAX</a> cabinets. This allowed me to select 4 IKEA standard sized doors to finish the cabinet with.</p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-luminous-vivid-orange-color has-text-color\"><strong>Related:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2020/10/fold-out-desk-home-office-pax.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Genius fold out home office desk in PAX wardrobe</a></p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<h5>Materials Required:</h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>2 <a href=\"https://fave.co/3eMfFkC\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">PAX Cabinets 238h x 100w x 58d</a> (unassembled)</li><li>4 doors</li><li><a href=\"https://amzn.to/3rTAu1b\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Decorative Cabinet Hardware</a></li><li>Folding Door Hardware</li><li>Next Bed Murphy Bed Kit (Queen Size 150 x 200cm)</li><li>1 IKEA closet rod insert set 500mm</li><li>4 Lag bolts 6mm</li><li>1 box 3.5 x 35mm screws</li><li>1 box 3.5 x 16mm screws</li><li>10 L-Brackets</li><li>7 white wood boards 6mm x 2mm x 2300m</li><li>Queen-sized memory foam mattress</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<h5>Tools Required:</h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>Hand Drill and Drill bits </li><li>Level</li><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://amzn.to/3ttOCP9\" target=\"_blank\">Miter Box and Saw</a></li><li><a href=\"https://amzn.to/3eT9gE3\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Carpenter’s Square</a></li><li>Screwdriver </li><li>Table saw</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<h5>Step 1</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Determine where you want the bed to be placed inside the cabinet. I despise living out of a suitcase when I travel, so I wanted to make sure our guests had a place to unpack and hang their clothes.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Included in the wardrobe, a hanging closet space and the bedside table on one side of my design. I positioned the bed to one side of the interior so that it left room for a small night table/cabinet plus hanging space on the opposite side. This is optional.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Step 2</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Secure your Next Bed Murphy bed frame to the wall. I have ceramic tile floors and baseboards, so I drilled through the baseboard tiles and used (4) 6mm lag bolts to secure my bed frame. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"480\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Attach-Next-Bed-floor-mounts.jpg\" alt=\"next bed murphy bed floor mounts\" class=\"wp-image-82662\"/></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Attach Next Bed floor mounts</p>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>Hint:</strong> Make sure you are using a ceramic drill bit to drill through ceramic tiles. I destroyed 4 porcelain drill bits before realizing I was using the wrong type of bit! Duh!</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Step 3</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Once you’ve determined your layout, cut the wood pieces for assembly. I don’t own a table saw, so I went to a local carpentry shop and paid them a few $ to cut the pieces for me. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Below is drawing I used to determine the cabinet layout, how each piece of the cabinet would be cut, and from where on the panel it would come from. Keep in mind that certain pieces of the IKEA cabinet are not finished on every edge. The shaded areas are discarded pieces.</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-gallery columns-2 is-cropped\"><ul class=\"blocks-gallery-grid\"><li class=\"blocks-gallery-item\"><figure><a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/layout-1.png\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"429\" height=\"503\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/layout-1.png\" alt=\"plan\" data-id=\"82664\" data-full-url=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/layout-1.png\" data-link=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/?attachment_id=82664\" class=\"wp-image-82664\"/></a></figure></li><li class=\"blocks-gallery-item\"><figure><a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/layout-2.png\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"467\" height=\"505\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/layout-2.png\" alt=\"plan\" data-id=\"82663\" data-full-url=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/layout-2.png\" data-link=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/?attachment_id=82663\" class=\"wp-image-82663\"/></a></figure></li></ul></figure>\n\n\n\n<h5>Cabinet pieces needed:</h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>Left Side 238 x 58cm</li><li>Right Side 238 x 58cm</li><li>Main Header 196 x 58cm</li><li>Plinth 196 x 8cm (finished edge)</li><li>Bottom Kick 196 x 8cm</li><li>Top Valance 196 x 8cm</li><li>Headboard 136 x 33cm</li><li>Shelf (3) 32 x 40 (one finished edge)</li><li>Closet 58 x 40 (two finished edges)</li><li>Side Table 48 x 40 (two finished edges)</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>I discovered during the cutting process that IKEA panels are not fully made out of MDF. Instead, they consist of an MDF frame with a waffle-like cardboard in between, all covered by a thin sheet of wood veneer.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Because of this newly discovered fact, I realized that I would need to build a support structure for the IKEA pieces to be attached to. I used 6mm x 2mm boards to create this.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Step 4</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Cut a notch into the bottom of the wall facing portion of each side piece so that they fit over the top of your floor molding, and sit flush with the wall.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Step 5</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Assemble a support frame for the main header piece of the cabinet using cut to size pieces of the 6mm x 2mm white wood board. I used the carpenter&#8217;s square to make sure everything is squared. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"506\" height=\"380\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/support-frame.png\" alt=\"support frame\" class=\"wp-image-82666\"/></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Support frame</p>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>Note:</strong> The support structure is hidden behind the decorative &#8220;wood&#8221; pieces, so you’ll need to take that into consideration when you’re cutting your support frame pieces to size.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>I built the support frame because the width of my cabinet is twice as wide as a normal IKEA cabinet, and has no support on the back to help bear the load of the main header. I also wanted to ensure the main header didn’t bow downward once the cabinet was assembled.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Step 6</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Attach the top valance piece to the front of the frame and secure the main header to this using 3.5 x 35mm screws. The screws are inserted from the structure into the valance piece so they don’t show once assembled. This photo shows the make-up of the material used in the construction of PAX cabinets.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"640\" height=\"480\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Attach-Valance.jpg\" alt=\"valance added\" class=\"wp-image-82665\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Attach-Valance.jpg 640w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Attach-Valance-550x413.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 640px) 100vw, 640px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Attach valance</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Step 7</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Secure the completed frame and valance to the top sides of the cabinet using 3.5 x 35mm screws.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Step 8</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Secure the main header to the header frame. I screwed the header board directly into the frame because I knew the weight of the board wouldn’t be supported if I screwed from the frame into the header in order to hide the screws. My screws are around the perimeter of the header board so even though they are exposed, they are not easily seen.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"640\" height=\"480\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Assembled-Cabinet.jpg\" alt=\"pax cabinet frame with support\" class=\"wp-image-82667\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Assembled-Cabinet.jpg 640w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Assembled-Cabinet-550x413.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 640px) 100vw, 640px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Assembled cabinet</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Because the back of the cabinet is completely open, I added a support for the bottom back of the cabinet and added two supports boards 100cm up to secure the headboard to.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Step 9 </h5>\n\n\n\n<p>(You’ll need two people for this step.)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Carefully lift the cabinet upright and attach the headboard by screwing from the back side through the two support boards into the headboard using 3.5 x 35mm screws.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Step 10</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>(Skip this step if you aren’t including the hanging closet and night table)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Position and secure the closet structure. I attached a leftover piece of 6mmm x 2mm to the inside roof of the cabinet as a hidden support inside the hanging closet and then cut decorative horizontal support boards from one of the unused trim pieces included the IKEA cabinet pack. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Because of the extra weight the closet would need to hold, I used L-brackets for additional support. I repeated the same idea to assemble the bed side table.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>If I did it over again, I would have created the bedside table first, and then the closet, and would have saved myself a few aches and pains from knocking my head into the closet while building the bedside table.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Step 11</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Secure a support board to the bottom front of the cabinet and attach the bottom kick and plinth to that support board. Afterwards, carefully shift the cabinet into place against the wall. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Once the cabinet was where I wanted it, I added an extra piece of support horizontally underneath the plinth to help bear the weight of the folding doors and the track the hardware runs on.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Step 12</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Secure the cabinet to the wall using lag screws and the securing hardware included in the IKEA Pax cabinet components. Use a level and square to make sure the cabinet is positioned evenly and squarely before securing it to the wall. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"480\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Completed-Cabinet-w-closet-and-night-table.jpg\" alt=\"pax cabinet done\" class=\"wp-image-82668\"/></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Completed cabinet with closet and night table</p>\n\n\n\n<p>My walls are concrete block, so I attached the cabinet to the wall just above the headboard. If you look at the photo closely, you can see the two black covers (one on each side) that IKEA includes in their cabinet securing hardware components.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Step 13</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Secure any artwork to the wall above the bed that you want to add.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"480\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Artwork-Added.jpg\" alt=\"added artwork\" class=\"wp-image-82669\"/></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h5>Step 14</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Assemble the Next Bed Murphy Bed Kit. I found the instructions for the Next Bed kit to be very clear and easy to follow. I would recommend having a can of WD40 close by to spray some of the areas of the components that you’ll need to slide into each other. It took me a total of 4 hours to fully assemble the bed kit.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"360\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Completed-Frame-in-Cabinet-up.jpg\" alt=\"next bed murphy bed installed\" class=\"wp-image-82670\"/></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"360\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Bed-Lowered.jpg\" alt=\"next bed murphy bed installed\" class=\"wp-image-82671\"/></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h5>Step 15</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Add your mattress. Murphy beds require a mattress that is able to stand on end without buckling or folding, so a memory foam mattress is the best recommendation.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"329\" height=\"437\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/with-mattress.png\" alt=\"memory foam mattress\" class=\"wp-image-82672\"/></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h5>Step 16</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Install door hardware. I purchased Hettich W-Line folding door hardware because I wanted as much of the cabinet interior to be exposed when the doors were open. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>This system uses a top and bottom guide for a really smooth movement. The instructions are vaguely written, and they seemed really complex, especially when calculating where to drill the hinge holes. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>I realized pretty quickly that I was over my head installing this type of system for the very first time.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Step 17</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Install wardrobe doors and decorative hardware. I ordered my IKEA doors in a standard white. Then, I contacted a cabinet maker in the area who agreed to paint them dark blue for a reasonable price. I purchased the <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://amzn.to/3rTAu1b\" target=\"_blank\">brass ring pulls on Amazon.com</a>. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>While the cabinet makers were delivering the freshly painted doors, I convinced them for a few extra $ to install the folding door hardware as I watched. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>I’m glad I did! </p>\n\n\n\n<p>The cost alone of purchasing the tools to complete the install myself would have been more than what I paid the professionals to do it for me.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Finished Project</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Overall, I am really pleased with how my Murphy Bed turned out. Our first guests arrive this weekend, so I look forward to hearing their feedback.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Finished-Project-3.jpg\" alt=\"next bed murphy bed installed in pax wardrobe\" class=\"wp-image-82673\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Finished-Project-3.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Finished-Project-3-550x733.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Finished-Project-2.jpg\" alt=\"next bed murphy bed installed in pax wardrobe\" class=\"wp-image-82674\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Finished-Project-2.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Finished-Project-2-550x733.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Finished-Project.jpg\" alt=\"next bed murphy bed installed in pax wardrobe\" class=\"wp-image-82675\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Finished-Project.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Finished-Project-550x733.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h5>Lessons learned</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Don’t get ahead of yourself. Before you position and secure the cabinet to the wall and add artwork, make sure that you have left enough clearance on each side of the cabinet for the sliding doors to open and for the bed to operate without any interference.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The internal hanging closet and night table are optional and add a level of complexity to the positioning of your bed within the cabinet. If you don’t need them, don’t include them in your project, and you’ll save yourself a few additional headaches along the way.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Total cost including labor for door painting and installation $1270. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Please note this price does not include the cost of the mattress or the Next Bed Murphy Bed kit.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>~ by Dennis Kight</p>\n</span><p>The post <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net\">IKEA Hackers</a>.</p>\n<div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/Ikeahacker?a=qWcpngrgTrU:7h-4TP8PnoY:yIl2AUoC8zA\"><img .jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn37@2020_3/2021/04/03/04-49-55-853_79a503bc5bfcce2e.webp","https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/with-mattress.png":null,"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Finished-Project-3.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn8@2020_4/2021/04/03/04-49-53-427_0658724de7221426.webp","https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Finished-Project-2.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn95@2020_1/2021/04/03/04-49-53-720_ad5083d4c7560a70.webp","https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Finished-Project.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn86@2020_3/2021/04/03/04-49-54-625_9ea9e1fcc92c403f.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/Ikeahacker?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn19@2020_4/2021/04/03/04-49-54-527_05353866f732d1c2.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/Ikeahacker?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx13/cdn71@2020_3/2021/04/03/04-49-53-457_1b4a6100740437d6.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/Ikeahacker?i=qWcpngrgTrU:7h-4TP8PnoY:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn16@2020_5/2021/04/03/04-49-53-427_bd8a55c77f6769aa.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/Ikeahacker/~4/qWcpngrgTrU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn62@2020_5/2021/04/03/04-49-53-968_99f2f707df593033.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1617425371954},{"createdTime":"2021-04-03 12:49:31","updatedTime":"2021-04-03 12:49:31","title":"“Colorful” RAST x 2 to Stacked MCM Dresser","link":"https://www.ikeahackers.net/?p=82750","description":"<span class=\"cb-itemprop\" itemprop=\"reviewBody\">\n<p class=\"has-medium-font-size\"><em>IKEA&#8217;s most affordable dresser goes MCM.</em></p>\n\n\n\n<p>My daughter and her partner had just moved back from England to Vancouver, Canada and had already spent a fortune on furniture basics for their very modern but small apartment.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Space in their bedroom was limited by sq. footage and because of two capacious built-ins on either side of the bed, even side tables wouldn&#8217;t work. And the one space they could put an additional piece of furniture without banging into it, near the foot of their bed, would only allow for a 12 inch depth, particularly if the dresser had drawers to pull out.<br><br>They had an IKEA TARVA headboard in unfinished pine and everything else was white. They liked the white/wood combo for a calm, inviting bedroom.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>So they were looking at an MCM dresser at <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://fave.co/3sKInXc\" target=\"_blank\">Wayfair</a> that cost $459 Cdn dollars. It had a white box frame and a few beech colored drawers, on angled legs. It was tall but narrow and 16” from the wall, so was still too deep.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>I was staying with them for a short while and thought I could go one better, with actual pine to match their bed. A better fit for depth and width, and save them $400.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Enter <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/tag/rast\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">RAST</a>. Two of them. Used, crayoned, battered but free, from Craigslist.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>These beauties before:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Double-Rast-Photo.jpg\" alt=\"rast chest of drawers\" class=\"wp-image-82751\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Double-Rast-Photo.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Double-Rast-Photo-550x413.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Double-Rast-Photo-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>I turned them into this stacked MCM dresser:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Unit-After-Photo.jpg\" alt=\"MCM dresser IKEA RAST hack\" class=\"wp-image-82752\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Unit-After-Photo.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Unit-After-Photo-550x733.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h5>IKEA item used: </h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li><a href=\"https://fave.co/31Tblsh\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">RAST chest of drawers</a> x 2</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"500\" height=\"500\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/06/IKEA-rast-chest-of-drawers.jpg\" alt=\"RAST chest of drawers\" class=\"wp-image-68499\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/06/IKEA-rast-chest-of-drawers.jpg 500w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/06/IKEA-rast-chest-of-drawers-150x150.jpg 150w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/06/IKEA-rast-chest-of-drawers-300x300.jpg 300w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/06/IKEA-rast-chest-of-drawers-50x50.jpg 50w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/06/IKEA-rast-chest-of-drawers-186x186.jpg 186w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\"><a href=\"https://fave.co/31Tblsh\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">RAST chest of drawers</a> | IKEA.com</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Tools and Supplies:</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>I had no power tools with me so this makeover was built almost entirely with what my daughter had on hand:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>Multi-head screwdriver</li><li>Hammer</li><li><a href=\"https://amzn.to/3wjaRcP\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Sandpaper on block</a></li><li>Paint brush, roller, tray</li><li>Level</li><li>Repurposed wood, nails &#38; screws from the RAST dressers themselves (Note, Dollarama is best source for cheap paint supplies if needed)</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>I bought in Cdn dollars:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li><a href=\"https://amzn.to/3fz2Z0G\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">PVA type wood glue</a> $5</li><li>Pale wood putty for pine $5</li><li>Primer 1 qt shellac-based $25 (best for unfinished pine)</li><li>Pure white satin paint 1 qt $18</li><li>4 corner brackets $5</li><li>3 flat brackets $2</li><li>A few longer screws $1</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>So the makeover without legs would have cost me $61 with tax. In the US, that cost would likely be less than $40 not only because of the exchange rate but because things are cheaper.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>I also bought the MCM legs and angled brackets for another $50 Cdn at <a href=\"https://fave.co/3dsP89F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Home Depot</a>. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Moreover, the kids are still deciding on new pulls so there will be a cost for those. Myself, I would have just spray painted the existing knobs in silver or brass for another $6.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>But as of now, total makeover including taxes and MCM legs is Canadian $111, and less than $80 US.</p>\n\n\n\n<h3>Steps to Stacked RAST MCM Dresser</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>1. Remove knobs, clean and sand everything down. I was only going to use four drawers of the six. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>So I kept back the two worst-crayoned ones, of which one drawer face was made into a shelf, and the backs of both of the drawers were used for side tables later. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Sanding was easy &#8211; 15 minutes. Don&#8217;t press hard. Then use a damp paper towel or tack cloth to remove wood dust.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>2. Construct the shape:</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>a) The Bottom:</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>The RAST bottom is hollow with just the two sides and a sunk back board at the front. I brought that board forward (outward) an inch or two, screwed it in on the sides, so it was flush with the front of the side boards, in order to achieve the boxy look I wanted.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>But I needed a proper bottom too in order to attach legs. There was an inner cross piece of wood further up the dresser that I removed. I glued, then screwed, this face-down on two of the discarded drawer sides, exactly squared off on the inner bottom, then screwed the crosspiece to the sides and the drawer pieces to the front piece.</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Bottom-of-Dresser-Photo-1.jpg\" alt=\"Bottom of Dresser \" class=\"wp-image-82754\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Bottom-of-Dresser-Photo-1.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Bottom-of-Dresser-Photo-1-550x413.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Bottom-of-Dresser-Photo-1-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>Very sturdy actually. This gave me the bottom. After painting I just screwed in the angled foot hardware in the four corners, then screwed the legs in.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>b) The Middle &#8211; Connecting the Dressers: </h5>\n\n\n\n<p>I removed the bottom front crosspiece from the second dresser, then stacked and glued the side legs to the first dresser. I reinforced this with 4 brackets on the inside of the top dresser&#8217;s legs connected to the bottom dresser&#8217;s top. Not ideal but I knew they would be painted over as to be hardly noticeable.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>c) The Shelf: </h5>\n\n\n\n<p>The top of the bottom dresser made one shelf with a high space that my daughter wanted. But I wanted another to lay across the top drawer of the bottom section. No piece was deep enough. However, the crosspiece I had removed from the top dresser, jutted up against a discarded drawer face, made a perfect sized shelf. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>So I glued these together and flat-bracketed them. I removed the plastic drawer slides I wasn&#8217;t using, then nailed a pair to the sides for the shelf to rest upon. These slides were originally inserted into premade holes, but are surprisingly sturdy enough when turned backwards and nailed, though awkwardly. You should have a level for this part. The back of my new shelf slid right in flush to the sides so I screwed that part to the frame for extra reinforcement.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>d) The Back: </h5>\n\n\n\n<p>The backs are thin pressboard and just nail tacked on but only cover half of each dresser. So I removed these and after painting them I re- tacked them to the back of the exposed shelving area, meeting behind the top shelf.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>And that was it for the build. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>None of the screwing or hammering was hard. I have little strength in my right wrist from a former fracture, so if I can do it so can you! And I spent a lot of time thinking about how to do all of this but only about an hour&#8217;s time actually doing it.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>3. Painting:</p>\n\n\n\n<p>a) Make sure all screws and nails that will show are fastened in as tight as possible. Then wood putty over them. Fill all holes with wood putty. In some deep cases you can fill with the wood glue first. Sand smooth with long strokes.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>b) Sand medium all surfaces to be painted. Clean dust with damp towel or tack cloth. Wait half hour always if you do use damp towel so dampness dries before applying primer or paint.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>c) Two coats of shellac-based primer. Follow instructions on can for drying times. Lightly sand, just tickle, between coats and clean as above.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>d) Two or three coats of paint. Before the final coat do a sand with the finest sandpaper you have, 220 or up is best.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>e) Apply a quick coat of clear, not amber, poly with rag for best results. But I didn&#8217;t have any, and they didn&#8217;t want it on the pine drawer faces anyway.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>f) Reinstall drawers, attach legs if not already, same with backs.<br>That might have been it except the RAST is a product that keeps on giving!</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Bedroom-Photo.jpg\" alt=\"MCM dresser IKEA RAST hack\" class=\"wp-image-82756\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Bedroom-Photo.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Bedroom-Photo-550x413.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Bedroom-Photo-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h5>Bonus side table</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Remember I said my daughter had no room for side tables because of the built-ins to either side?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>I had two solid drawer backs left so I just laid them inside each built-in drawer, over their clothes, and stabilized them with Command poster strips on the inner ridge. Now they have somewhere to rest a cup of coffee and a book! And their drawers still close &#8212; sans coffee cup of course!</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Side-Table-Photo.jpg\" alt=\"side table\" class=\"wp-image-82755\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Side-Table-Photo.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Side-Table-Photo-550x413.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Side-Table-Photo-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h5>Time spent: </h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>Thinking: At least 8-16 hours!</li><li>Constructing: 1 hour</li><li>Prepping: putty, sanding etc: 1 hour</li><li>Priming and painting, not incl wait times: 2 hours</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>So it seems a lot but I did all the thinking for you! 4 hours and $111 or less than $80 US. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Including tax my daughter saved $400 and got a better-suited and better-fitting MCM dresser, made of wood not laminate. Not to mention side tables! Fan-rast-ic!</p>\n\n\n\n<p>From this:</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Double-Rast-Photo.jpg\" alt=\"rast chest of drawers\" class=\"wp-image-82751\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Double-Rast-Photo.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Double-Rast-Photo-550x413.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Double-Rast-Photo-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>To this:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Unit-After-Photo.jpg\" alt=\"MCM dresser IKEA RAST hack\" class=\"wp-image-82752\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Unit-After-Photo.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/Unit-After-Photo-550x733.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h5>Would I do it again? </h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Likely only if I had similar space limitations. The RAST is the only suitable dresser I found at 12” depth. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>But I find the plastic slides cheap and stacking was harder and more costly than I thought. So was painting unfinished pine because of the priming and more costly shellac-based primer. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>There were a lot of holes to fill. These pieces were battered! </p>\n\n\n\n<p>I’ve stained a lot of furniture and painted over painted furniture and both were far easier and cheaper than this RAST MCM dresser project. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>But I enjoyed it all thoroughly so who knows?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>~ by Barbara Curtis</p>\n</span><p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" on your plate too.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>IKEA Canada is helping us rethink food waste with&#160;<em>Scrapsbook</em>, a new cookbook that turns bottom-of-the-crisper vegetables, overripe fruit and what we&#8217;ll normally toss in the bin into edible &#8212; more importantly &#8212; delicious meals. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img It includes breakfast, mains, soups and dessert ideas. Chefs specialising in diverse cuisines like Adrian Forte, Craig Wong, and Trevor Bird have contributed to the beautifully photographed cookbook. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>For breakfast, tuck into Banana Peel Bacon &#38; Wild Rice Pancakes made from leftover rice and banana peel.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"690\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ikea-scraps-book-cookbook-5.png\" alt=\"ikea scrapsbook food scraps cookboo\" class=\"wp-image-82697\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ikea-scraps-book-cookbook-5.png 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ikea-scraps-book-cookbook-5-550x371.png 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ikea-scraps-book-cookbook-5-768x518.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-luminous-vivid-orange-color has-text-color\"><strong>Related:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2020/04/ikea-meatball-recipe.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IKEA shares meatball recipe so you can have it at home</a></p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<p>Then for lunch, we recommend the Corn Husk Smoked Chicken. With this dish, you&#8217;ll milk the last bit of goodness from corn hobs. Serve garnished with a web of corn silk. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"689\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ikea-scraps-book-cookbook-4.png\" alt=\"ikea scrapsbook food scraps cookboo\" class=\"wp-image-82695\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ikea-scraps-book-cookbook-4.png 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ikea-scraps-book-cookbook-4-550x370.png 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ikea-scraps-book-cookbook-4-768x517.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Dinner is pulp burgers with DIY jalapeño cheese. This should effectively clean out the pulp, vegetable scraps, and skins you&#8217;ve been saving.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The recipes are eye opening and definitely challenges what we perceive as waste. waste-saving tips, and of course, IKEA dining products, plates and bowls to complete the meal.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>IKEA Canada customers can enter an <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" 12:49:31","updatedTime":"2021-04-03 12:49:31","title":"IKEA FYRTUR wireless blind: Switching from battery to permanent power supply","link":"https://www.ikeahackers.net/?p=82680","description":"<span class=\"cb-itemprop\" itemprop=\"reviewBody\">\n<p>I have mounted an IKEA&#160;FYRTUR wireless roller blind in a position, where it is difficult to get access to the battery chamber to recharge the battery. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>So I decided to replace the battery with a Universal Power Supply. The process turned out to be rather simple.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>IKEA item used:</h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://fave.co/3cTZJKD\" target=\"_blank\">FYRTUR wireless roller blind</a></li><li>5. 7,5V DC Universal Power Supply</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"459\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-blind-1.jpg\" alt=\"ikea fyrtur wireless blind\" class=\"wp-image-82687\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-blind-1.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-blind-1-550x247.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-blind-1-768x344.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><a href=\"https://fave.co/3cTZJKD\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"509\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-blind-2.jpg\" alt=\"ikea fyrtur wireless blind\" class=\"wp-image-82688\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-blind-2.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-blind-2-550x273.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-blind-2-768x382.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></a></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Credit: <a href=\"https://fave.co/3cTZJKD\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IKEA.com</a></p>\n\n\n\n<h3>Battery operated IKEA FYRTUR blinds to direct power supply</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>1. In an electrical store, I found a Universal Power Supply with variable voltage output, among which was 7,5V DC (2.25 A). It was close enough to replace the standard battery rated to 7.2V DC. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Price around 20 €. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/usb-power.jpg\" alt=\"universal power supply\" class=\"wp-image-82681\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/usb-power.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/usb-power-550x550.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/usb-power-150x150.jpg 150w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/usb-power-768x768.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/usb-power-125x125.jpg 125w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>2. Remove 4 screws at the angular battery cover upper left side of the FYRTUR chassis. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-power.jpeg\" alt=\"battery cover\" class=\"wp-image-82682\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-power.jpeg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-power-550x413.jpeg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-power-768x576.jpeg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-luminous-vivid-orange-color has-text-color\"><strong>Related:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2020/05/ikea-kadrilj-motorized-blinds.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">How to extend the new IKEA KADRILJ motorized blinds</a></p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<p>3. Use a thin piece of metal to loosen the angular part at the left end of the chassis. Carefully lift the cover upward. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-power-2.jpeg\" alt=\"battery cover\" class=\"wp-image-82683\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-power-2.jpeg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-power-2-550x733.jpeg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>4. Remove the battery.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>5. Drill a small hole for the wire into the battery chamber. 7-8 mm may fit. I made the hole in the battery hatch, but you can also place it elsewhere to allow the wire to connect to the battery contact plug. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-power-3.jpeg\" alt=\"chassis\" class=\"wp-image-82684\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-power-3.jpeg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-power-3-550x413.jpeg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-power-3-768x576.jpeg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>6. Draw out the battery chamber. On its left side there is the battery contact plug with 4 legs. You will only use only the two outermost pins. Looking at the backside of the battery plus you can see two wires: a white (-) and a red (+). It is difficult to connect the wire from the power supply here. Use instead the pins at the inside, but note where the red wire is connected as this must receive + 7,5V. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-power-4.jpeg\" alt=\"ikea fyrtur wireless roller blind with permanent power supply\" class=\"wp-image-82685\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-power-4.jpeg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-power-4-550x413.jpeg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-power-4-768x576.jpeg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h5>Reassemble</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>7. Pull the cord through your hole in the battery chamber and solder the two wires to the outermost pins in the battery chamber. In most cases the positive wire from power supply will be marked with a white stripe in the black isolation. This wire must be soldered, so it connect to the red wire on the backside. If in doubt use a voltmeter to check.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-power-5.jpeg\" alt=\"ikea fyrtur wireless roller blind with permanent power supply\" class=\"wp-image-82686\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-power-5.jpeg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-power-5-550x413.jpeg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/fyrtur-power-5-768x576.jpeg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>8. Now assemble the battery chamber and its hatch in the chassis again in reverse order. Be careful to insert the small round pin, which functions as a shaft for the hatch.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Now you don’t need to care about recharging the battery in FYRTUR any more.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>~ by Mogens Brun</p>\n</span><p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2021/03/ikea-fyrtur-direct-power-supply.html\">IKEA FYRTUR wireless blind: Switching from battery to permanent power
