DK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx13/cdn71@2020_3/2021/04/03/04-49-53-457_1b4a6100740437d6.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/Ikeahacker?i=xVg_sskG9C4:e8kzD9eT2QM:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn70@2020_4/2021/04/03/04-49-54-157_b934f08b3f753d77.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/Ikeahacker/~4/xVg_sskG9C4":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx31/cdn32@2020_3/2021/04/03/04-49-53-356_1fe1a9cef58a5bd0.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1617425371953},{"createdTime":"2021-04-03 12:49:31","updatedTime":"2021-04-03 12:49:31","title":"Moppe got his stripes with infusible ink transfer sheets","link":"https://www.ikeahackers.net/?p=82726","description":"<span class=\"cb-itemprop\" itemprop=\"reviewBody\">\n<p>This wooden thing &#8212; the <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/tag/moppe\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">MOPPE mini chest of drawers</a> &#8212; had been sitting in my <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2020/02/craft-room-ideas-ikea-hacks.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">craft room</a> for years begging for a makeover. But I didn&#8217;t want to paint it because of the possibility of the drawers getting harder to pull out.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>I used infusible ink transfer sheets instead. All in all, an easy makeover for the MOPPE.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-11a.jpg\" alt=\"Moppe wooden chest with infusible ink transfer sheets\" class=\"wp-image-82733\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-11a.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-11a-550x413.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-11a-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h5>IKEA items used: </h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li><a href=\"https://fave.co/3cC6qAA\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IKEA MOPPE mini chest of drawers</a></li></ul>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"495\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-chest.jpg\" alt=\"moppe chest\" class=\"wp-image-82731\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-chest.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-chest-550x266.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-chest-768x371.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Photo: IKEA.com</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Other materials and tools:</h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li><a href=\"https://amzn.to/3cBQekb\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Cricut infusible ink transfer sheets</a></li><li><a href=\"https://amzn.to/3rLuCGB\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Heat press</a> or iron</li><li>Scissors or plotter</li><li>Heat proof tape</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<h3>How to use Cricut infusible ink transfer sheets on wood: </h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Measure your placement and plan your design.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-13_a.jpg\" alt=\"cricut infusible ink transfer sheets\" class=\"wp-image-82738\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-13_a.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-13_a-550x413.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-13_a-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Cut out your design in the print sheet.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-2_a.jpg\" alt=\"lay out the design\" class=\"wp-image-82727\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-2_a.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-2_a-550x733.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-luminous-vivid-orange-color has-text-color\"><strong>Related:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2020/07/half-this-to-make-an-ikea-moppe-alternative.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Half this to make an IKEA MOPPE alternative</a></p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<p>Place the design, face down on the wood. Tape it in place.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Lay parchment paper on top of design. (Included in the <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://amzn.to/3cBQekb\" target=\"_blank\">infusible ink transfer sheets package</a>.)</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-5_a.jpg\" alt=\"Cricut easypress\" class=\"wp-image-82728\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-5_a.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-5_a-550x733.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Heat a <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://amzn.to/3rLuCGB\" target=\"_blank\">heat press</a> to 205 degrees Celsius (approx. 400 degrees F). Carefully place press on top of parchment paper and with no pressure let it sit for 60 seconds. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-3_a.jpg\" alt=\"Moppe wooden chest with infusible ink transfer sheets\" class=\"wp-image-82729\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-3_a.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-3_a-550x733.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Watch it and if there are signs of smoke, remove right away.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>After 60 sec carefully remove press and let the design cool. Don&#8217;t move anything.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>After it has cooled. Remove the sheet and behold your transfer!</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-12_a.jpg\" alt=\"Moppe wooden chest with infusible ink transfer sheets\" class=\"wp-image-82730\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-12_a.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-12_a-550x413.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-12_a-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-a.jpg\" alt=\"Moppe wooden chest with infusible ink transfer sheets\" class=\"wp-image-82732\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-a.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-a-550x413.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/moppe-cricut-a-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h5>How long and how much did it cost?</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>It took me 45 min from start to finish. I bought the infusible ink transfer sheets for 14 euro. The other stuff I already had at home as mad crafter. </p>\n\n\n\n<h5>What do you like most about the hack?</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Now this piece looks like me! It&#8217;s not bland. It&#8217;s fun and invites to conversation and usage.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>What was the hardest part about this hack?</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Figuring out if the wood would catch fire. The was a bit of research involved.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>What to pay special attention to?</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Not shifting the design as it will leave shadows.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Looking back, would you have done it differently?</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Using more tape to secure the design. There are many different designs of the sheets to choose from so you can really make this your own. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>~ by <a href=\"http://www.instagram.com/elfmakes\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Emma Lanner Frånlund</a> from Sweden</p>\n</span><p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2021/03/infusible-ink-transfer-sheets-on-wood.html\">Moppe got his stripes with infusible ink transfer sheets</a> appeared first on <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net\">IKEA Hackers</a>.</p>\n<div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a itemprop=\"reviewBody\">\n<p>The IKEA HEMNES sideboard was chipped and looking shabby after an international move. At the same time, our kitchen table and chairs were equally shabby. So we replaced them with this IKEA HEMNES kitchen peninsula hack and countertop stools.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1080\" height=\"1080\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/hemnes-kitchen-peninsula.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA HEMNES kitchen peninsula hack\" class=\"wp-image-82717\" https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/hemnes-kitchen-peninsula-125x125.jpg 125w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1080px) 100vw, 1080px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-luminous-vivid-orange-color has-text-color\"><strong>Related:</strong> <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2013/05/glass-top-kitchen-peninsula.html\" target=\"_blank\">IVAR cabinets for a glass top kitchen peninsula</a></p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<h5>IKEA items and other materials:</h5>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"478\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/hemnes-sideboard-1.png\" alt=\"ikea hemnes\" class=\"wp-image-82718\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/hemnes-sideboard-1.png 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/hemnes-sideboard-1-550x257.png 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/hemnes-sideboard-1-768x359.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Photo: <a href=\"https://fave.co/3cimwRa\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IKEA.com</a></p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://fave.co/3cimwRa\" target=\"_blank\">IKEA HEMNES sideboard</a> (bought pre-loved, approx 50 USD)</li><li>Paint and varnish (approx 10 USD)</li><li>Custom made stained wood top (approx 100 USD)</li><li>Sandpaper </li></ul>\n\n\n\n<h3>Turning the IKEA HEMNES into a kitchen peninsula</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>First, we sanded the assembled HEMNES sideboard. Then, painted it with several coats of Jotun Silk Sea Emerald. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>I painted three coats of emulsion and a two coats of varnish over 3 days, letting the paint fully dry before the varnish.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Once I got the custom-made stained worktop I placed it on top of the HEMNES sideboard, adjusting the overhang to where I want it to be. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Then, drilled four screws from under the top of the HEMNES sideboard into the wood of the worktop. We drilled at each corner of the HEMNES, from beneath. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/hemnes-to-peninsula-1.jpg\" alt=\"kitchen peninsula hack\" class=\"wp-image-82715\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/hemnes-to-peninsula-1.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/hemnes-to-peninsula-1-550x413.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/hemnes-to-peninsula-1-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>The countertop is very heavy and doesn&#8217;t move when placed on the HEMNES. But as a precaution, (I have kids), I screwed it in because I didn&#8217;t want it to tip.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The worktop measures 160cm x 75cm. The countertop overhangs on one side more than the other so the drawers can be accessed.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/hemnes-to-peninsula-2.jpg\" alt=\"kitchen peninsula diy\" class=\"wp-image-82716\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/hemnes-to-peninsula-2.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/hemnes-to-peninsula-2-550x413.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/hemnes-to-peninsula-2-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Lastly, we moved the the HEMNES peninsula into position And that was it. </p>\n\n\n\n<h5>What do you like most about the hack?</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>The colour. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>I think I will get the stool tops replaced with the same wood as the counter top.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>What to pay special attention to?</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Seal every part with varnish since it is being used in a kitchen/wet area.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Looking back, would you have done it differently?</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>I would have made the top slightly wider &#8212; it is now 75cm × 160cm. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>~ Bridgee Dunn </p>\n</span><p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" itemprop=\"reviewBody\">\n<p>JoepW finds a way to maximize the 20cm wide <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/tag/maximera\" target=\"_blank\">MAXIMERA</a> pull-out spice cabinet to store even more spice jars. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>As the cabinet has only 2 levels, it leaves a lot of usable space above the short spice jars. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/maximera-spice-drawer-4.jpg\" alt=\"maximera pull out interior fittings\" class=\"wp-image-82609\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/maximera-spice-drawer-4.jpg 768w, is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-luminous-vivid-orange-color has-text-color\"><strong>Related:</strong> <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2016/07/easy-peasy-spice-drawer.html\" target=\"_blank\">Easy peasy spice drawer</a></p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<p>Furthermore, Joep found the tapered sides that hide the runners pretty clumsy. They do not allow you to put a lot of items next to each other, or it will wedge against the tapered sides and easily tip over. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>This is especially true for the nice round glass spices containers he had envisioned to store in it.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>And so a hack was needed.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>IKEA item used: </h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://fave.co/30wigGS\" target=\"_blank\">MAXIMERA pull out interior fitting</a></li></ul>\n\n\n\n<h5>Other materials:</h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>Aluminium sheet</li><li>Small foldable crate</li><li>Corner brackets</li><li><a href=\"https://amzn.to/3l0aheC\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Plastic angle brackets</a></li></ul>\n\n\n\n<h5>#1 Adding an angled shelf for spices</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Joep folded an aluminium sheet to roughly follow the contours of the spice containers. One row of containers stands upright on a shelf, the other row lays at an angle. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/maximera-spice-drawer-3.jpg\" alt=\"angled spice shelf\" class=\"wp-image-82605\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/maximera-spice-drawer-3.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/maximera-spice-drawer-3-550x413.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/maximera-spice-drawer-3-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>With some corner brackets he screwed the two shelves to the front panel and rear pole just underneath the top drawer. And voilà! Two new rows of spices nicely lined up between the top and bottom drawer. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/maximera-spice-drawer-2.jpg\" alt=\"pull out spice cabinet\" class=\"wp-image-82606\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/maximera-spice-drawer-2.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/maximera-spice-drawer-2-550x413.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/maximera-spice-drawer-2-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-luminous-vivid-orange-color has-text-color\"><strong>Related:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2018/02/spice-organizer-two-ikea-spice-racks.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Spice Organizer from two IKEA spice racks</a></p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<h5>#2 Adding another level of storage</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Another addition happened when he found foldable crates that were just the right width as the pull out drawer. With a bit of <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3rzXzWm\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">hot glue</a> and <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3l0aheC\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">plastic angle pieces</a>, these crates sit nice and snug on top of the drawer to allow for even more storage. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/maximera-spice-drawer.jpg\" alt=\"foldable crate\" class=\"wp-image-82607\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/maximera-spice-drawer.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/maximera-spice-drawer-550x413.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/maximera-spice-drawer-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>And you can slide them forward and backward to access the spices underneath. Or remove them completely should you not require them anymore.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/maximera-spice-drawer-5.jpg\" alt=\"pull out spice cabinet\" class=\"wp-image-82608\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/maximera-spice-drawer-5.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/maximera-spice-drawer-5-550x413.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/maximera-spice-drawer-5-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>With these two addition, Joep&#8217;s pull-out spice cabinet is duly maxed out.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>See the <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://www.instructables.com/IkeaHack-Maximizing-the-Maximera/\" itemprop=\"reviewBody\">\n<p>I needed to build a leg rest due to an injury my son had. Due to this circumstance, I needed to be creative in building a leg support for his injured leg.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>And we had an old FROSTA stool around.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/leg-rest-1.jpg\" alt=\"fractured tibia DIY leg rest\" is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-luminous-vivid-orange-color has-text-color\"><strong>Related:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2018/04/garden-bar-cart-outdoor-entertaining.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Hack a Garden Bar Cart for outdoor entertaining</a></p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<h5>IKEA Item used:</h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>1 x <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/tag/frosta\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">FROSTA stool</a></li></ul>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"500\" height=\"500\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/10/ikea-frosta-wooden-stool.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA FROSTA sizes=\"(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Photo: IKEA.com</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Other Materials and tools: </h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>10x Countersunk screw</li><li>2 x screw hook</li><li>2 x washer</li><li>1m <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://amzn.to/3ddF8Ru\" target=\"_blank\">lashing strap</a></li><li>20 x <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://amzn.to/3dg2feb\" target=\"_blank\">eyelets</a></li><li>1 x wood panel 400mmx260mmx27mm</li><li>Saw</li><li>Drill press</li><li>Sanding paper</li><li>Electric drill</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<h3>Leg rest instruction:</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>We used the four legs of the FROSTA stool for this hack. If you have it assembled, unscrew the legs from the seat. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Shorten the legs according to the plan <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://tognella.com/en/2021/03/17/ikea-live-hack-leg-rest-from-frosta-stool/\" target=\"_blank\">here</a>. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Get a wooden base plate and attach the FROSTA legs to the wood. You will need to make new holes for this. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>On the A side of legs, add screw hooks to the top of the legs.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/leg-rest-1.jpeg\" alt=\"fractured tibia DIY leg rest\" class=\"wp-image-82724\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/leg-rest-1.jpeg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/leg-rest-1-550x733.jpeg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-luminous-vivid-orange-color has-text-color\"><strong>Related:</strong> <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2014/12/frosta-half-shelves.html\" target=\"_blank\">Wall mounted half circle shelves</a></p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<p>Then, get ready 4 strips of <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://amzn.to/3ddF8Ru\" target=\"_blank\">lashing straps</a> at 50 cm each. These are available from the DIY store. Hammer in <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://amzn.to/3dg2feb\" target=\"_blank\">eyelets</a> at a distance of 2cm. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>On one end of the strap, put in a 4×40 screw with washer and screw it into the top of the B side of the legs.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The leg rest is now ready to be used.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Our son has made good use of it and it has taken a lot of pain away from him as it provides a flexible and comfortable support.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>How long did it take?</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Build time was about 1 hour. And it cost about 100 CHF excluding the FROSTA stool which I already had.  </p>\n\n\n\n<h5>What do you like the most about the hack?</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>I like the flexibility of the leg rest.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>See the <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://tognella.com/en/2021/03/17/ikea-live-hack-leg-rest-from-frosta-stool\" target=\"_blank\">full instructions here</a>.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>~ by Patrick Tognella</p>\n</span><p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2021/03/fractured-tibia-leg-rest.html\">Tibia Fracture Leg Rest from old </h3>\n\n\n\n<p>I wanted something simple and easy to put together without too much carpentry skills required.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>It all started with a <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/tag/billy\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">BILLY</a> bookshelf 80x28x106.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>It is very simple to create because you don&#8217;t need many tools, except a cordless drill or screwdriver.</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1004\" height=\"1338\" shelves if your BILLY bookshelf is already assembled. Then, coated the entire parts inside the BILLY bookshelf with <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://amzn.to/3cdb0GM\" target=\"_blank\">brick-like peel and stick adhesive stickers</a>. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>I used one of the shelf for the top panel, fixed with L brackets to the lateral part of the BILLY.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Then, I used white wood panel for the two sides. I fixed them with screws and L brackets to the sides of the BILLY bookshelf. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1004\" height=\"1338\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/billy-fireplace-4.jpg\" alt=\"decorative fireplace ikea billy hack\" class=\"wp-image-82705\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/billy-fireplace-4.jpg 1004w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/billy-fireplace-4-550x733.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/billy-fireplace-4-768x1023.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1004px) 100vw, 1004px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Next, I attached the molding around the BILLY panels using glue.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Lastly, I finished it off with a larger wood panel for the mantel.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1000\" height=\"749\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/billy-fireplace-2a.jpg\" alt=\"decorative fireplace ikea billy hack\" class=\"wp-image-82706\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/billy-fireplace-2a.jpg 1000w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/billy-fireplace-2a-550x412.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/billy-fireplace-2a-768x575.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Set decorations inside the fireplace. All to fuel an extensive refurbishment of a run-down Victorian farmhouse we bought. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>One of the things we saw were washing machines and tumblers on a laundry pedestal. But we couldn’t afford the custom joinery to get them built – IKEA to the rescue!</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Before and After!</h5>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"708\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/before_after.jpg\" alt=\"before after: laundry pedestal with drawer\" class=\"wp-image-82614\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/before_after.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/before_after-550x380.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/before_after-768x531.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h5>IKEA items used:</h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li><a href=\"https://fave.co/3lbcvrW\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">METOD frames</a>:<ul><li>60&#215;100 wall unit with 2 x VOXTORP beige doors</li><li>60&#215;40 wall unit with VOXTORP door</li><li>Corner sink unit with VOXTORP door</li><li>30&#215;60 base unit with VOXTORP door</li></ul></li><li>2 x METOD/MAXIMERA 60&#215;60 2-drawer sink units with VOXTORP doors</li><li>2 x METOD 60&#215;40 fridge-freezer top cabinets with VOXTORP doors</li><li>Various VOXTORP cover panels</li><li>1 x VOXTORP plinth</li><li>1 x VOXTORP déco strip</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<h5>Other materials:</h5>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>2 x B&#38;Q white breakfast bar worktops</li><li>1 x B&#38;Q white worktop</li><li>1 x existing sink</li><li>38x64mm timber and metal brackets</li><li>18mm plywood</li><li>25mm Wickes nickel clothes rail and brackets</li><li>4 bags floor screed compound</li><li>2 x sets of garage wall foam door protectors from eBay</li><li>Circular saw</li><li>Jigsaw</li><li>Drill/driver</li><li>Screwdriver</li><li>Framing square</li><li>Spirit level</li><li>Assorted screws, <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3eA8dJ8\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">No More Nails adhesive</a> and caulk</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<h3>Laundry pedestal with drawers</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>The key thing to achieve was to sit the appliances on a platform so they’d be at waist height and much easier to load and unload. I wanted a laundry basket to sit on a shelf in front of the washing machine or tumbler to easily load and unload the machines. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>I knew regular kitchen units wouldn’t take the load and vibrations of a washing machine and tumbler, but thought I could construct a basic timber frame that would be strong enough.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The original scullery had been a utility room, but was in a pretty poor state. When we got our kitchen refurbished we asked the plasterer to re-skim the utility room walls. We also needed to secure some of the old quarry tiles by cementing them back in place and then I laid a screed over the top to level the floor.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Here’s the floor units for the sink in their rough position. And the first of the METOD/MAXIMERA units in place to get measurements for the frame after the room had been replastered and screeded.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-new-floor-units.jpg\" alt=\"metod frames\" class=\"wp-image-82615\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-new-floor-units.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-new-floor-units-550x413.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-new-floor-units-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-luminous-vivid-orange-color has-text-color\"><strong>Related:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2015/12/ikea-besta-media-center-washer-dryer-hack-pedestal.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IKEA BESTÅ media center is now a washer/dryer pedestal</a></p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-wide\"/>\n\n\n\n<p>Because the sink units I was using for the appliance platform only have two metal strips over the top, they’re easy to cut down to the desired height and reattach the metal strips to the top of the shortened side panels.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Construction the pedestal frame</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>Next was constructing the frame to support the appliances. I used standard studwork timber, braced with brackets from B&#38;Q. Each end of the frame was screwed into the floor. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>I thought 40mm worktop on top of this would probably be strong enough.  But just to make sure there’d be no flexing and bouncing, I decided to add an 18mm plywood board to support the middle. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Below, you can just about make out the pencil lines marked on the floor for where it’s going to go. I was planning on covering the front of the timber frame with cut down VOXTORP cover panels, so figured I’d just cut another very slim strip to cover the front of the plywood too.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-frame.jpg\" alt=\"framing\" class=\"wp-image-82616\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-frame.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-frame-550x733.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Here’s the platform constructed and the appliances in place. Also testing the all-important MAXIMERA drawer to take a standard laundry basket. You can also see the wall units in place.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-frame-with-drawers.jpg\" alt=\"laundry pedestal with drawer\" class=\"wp-image-82617\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-frame-with-drawers.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-frame-with-drawers-550x733.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>At this point, I tested the washing machine with a load. The platform was strong enough, but on the spin cycle there was a lot of lateral movement I hadn’t anticipated! </p>\n\n\n\n<p>I’d already planned to build a shelf over our floor-mounted boiler to the left, which would screw into the tall end panel on the right of the platform and brace that side. </p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Reinforcing against lateral movement</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>To add some stability on the other side, I screwed the end panel to the sink worktop, knowing the screws would be hidden by the tumbler. The timber frame below is also screwed to the corner unit, which is screwed to the wall, so this side was pretty solid.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-panel-fix-to-worktop.jpg\" alt=\"utility panel fix to worktop\" class=\"wp-image-82618\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-panel-fix-to-worktop.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-panel-fix-to-worktop-550x413.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-panel-fix-to-worktop-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Then I cut the worktop for the boiler shelf, screwing that through the other end panel and securing the other end on a timber batten attached to the wall.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-boiler-shelf.jpg\" alt=\"utility boiler shelf\" class=\"wp-image-82619\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-boiler-shelf.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-boiler-shelf-550x413.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-boiler-shelf-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>With the studwork timber frame and plywood support below, the appliance platform was about 60mm wider than the combined width of the appliances. The wall units above are on a standard IKEA suspension rail and it was easy enough to cut a cover panel to use as a central spacer. They’re also screwed to the end panels for a little extra strength and stability.</p>\n\n\n\n<h5>Adding stability</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>To make sure the washing machine couldn’t go anywhere during the spin cycle, I found some self-adhesive firm foam panels on eBay. These are intended to stick on garage walls and protect your car doors when opening.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>When stuck on the sides of the washer and tumbler and squeezed into my laundry pedestal, they provided the perfect spacers. I squeezed a strip of 6mm ply in the middle to add some additional force to the sides and I can confirm that our washing machine on a 1400rpm spin with a full load now doesn’t move anywhere!</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-foam.jpg\" alt=\"utility foam\" class=\"wp-image-82620\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-foam.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-foam-550x733.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h5>Laundry basket shelves</h5>\n\n\n\n<p>The final step was then making my laundry basket shelves. The MAXIMERA sink units come with two sets of drawer runners. I used the bottom pair exactly as shown in the cabinet instructions to take the standard drawer. This is the perfect size to take a standard round UK laundry basket.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>I then fitted the second pair in the top of my cut down cabinets and cut a piece of cover panel to size to use as a shelf and just glued it on to the runners. I also drilled a finger hole in the shelf, so you can easily pull out the shelf when you’re ready to load or unload a machine.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-basket-shelf-1.jpg\" alt=\"laundry pedestal with drawer for basket and pull out shelf\" class=\"wp-image-82621\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-basket-shelf-1.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-basket-shelf-1-550x733.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>So the drawers each store a laundry basket, and you simply pull it out and sit it on the shelf when you need to take a load out of the machine. For a little extra stability with a full basket, we’ve started to close the drawer slightly so the drawer front supports the front of the basket, and that works a treat.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-basket-shelf-2.jpg\" alt=\"laundry pedestal with drawer\" class=\"wp-image-82622\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-basket-shelf-2.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-basket-shelf-2-550x733.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>So there you go – our utility room has gone from a horrible mess to a really functional space where we don’t ever have to bend down to load or unload a machine. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-finished-2.jpg\" alt=\"laundry pedestal with drawer\" class=\"wp-image-82623\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-finished-2.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/utility-finished-2-550x733.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>The hacking of the IKEA sink units is really easy, and if you have some basic joinery skills you’ll be able to make a similar laundry pedestal that works just as well.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>~ by Chris Perkins</p>\n</span><p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\"
